 chaahe yah ek nijee bank ho yaa saarvajanik kshetra kaa bank, koi bhi bhartiya sarkaar yaa arabiai aisi sthiti main nahin rahanaa chahega jahaan koi bank unki najaron ke saamne gadbaditaan karata jaae
 Whenever the central bank finds out any reason for a problem in a bank, it immediately takes corrective action to rectify it as it did in the case of Lakshmi Vilas Bank
 yadi sthiti main sudhaar nahin hota, to arabiai aamtaur par use kisi majboot bank ke saath vilay kii suvidha detaa he
 In recent times, RBI did the same when Global Trust Bank (a small private bank) saw it in crisis and merged it with Oriental Bank of Commerce, a PSU bank
 chakravarti kehete hai, ''aakhirkaar agar kisi aniyantrit chook ke kaaran banking patan kii ore badhata he, to nijee or saarvajanik kshetra, donon tarah ke bank nistaaran yojana ke tahat kendriya bank kii karrwai ke adheen honge
 Presently, whether it is a merger or acquisition, the risk is the same for the deposit holders
 '' beshak, satark rahane kii jarurat hoti he
 "the level of security among banks varies depending on their financial position," says Minna Aggarwal, financial educator, money mentor and founder of Finsphe
 ucchtar enpie or kam puunji paryaptata anupaat vaale bainkon se bachaa janaa chahie
 "with a co-operative bank, is your money safe? All commercial banks, be it public sector or private sector, are directly governed by RBI
" lekin jab sahakaari bainkon kii baat aati he, to unke paas dohare viniman hote hai
 Apart from RBI, they are also regulated by the respective registrars of central or various state cooperative societies under which they are registered
 paisabazardotcom ke siio or sah-sansthaapak naveen kukereja kehete hai, ''korporate gavarnence or vyavsaayikta kii kami sahakaari bainkon ke kamjor swasthya ke mukhya kaaran hai
 Dual regulation also gives way for urban cooperative banks (ucbs) like PMC Bank to avoid detection of irregularities
 sahakaari bainkon main peshewar board nahin hote kyonki unke nideshak mandal sidhe bank ke sadasyon dwaara chune jate hai
 Unlike commercial banks, cooperative banks do not require RBI approval while appointing a chief executive
 ''kukereja kehete hai, ''jahaan tak in bainkon ke viniman kaa sambandh he, arabiai saamaanya banking kaaryon ko niyantrit karata he jabaki sahakaari samitiyon ke register in bainkon ke prashasan or lekha pariksha ko viniyamit karte hai
 This double control leaves some flaws in the regulatory framework

 Almost all banks have this facility under which depositors get insurance cover on deposits up to Rs 1 lakh which can include both principal and interest
 kukereja kehete hai, ''bank ke vifal ho jane par yah beemaa 1 lakh rupye tak kii bank jamaa raashi ko cover karata he, jisamen har jamakarta kii saavadhi, bachat, chaalu or aavarti jamaa shaamil hai
 There is no difference in the level of security of deposits in any type of bank covered and covered under the Deposit Insurance and Credit Guarantee Corporation (DICGC)
 diisijisi ek arabiai ke purna swaamitv vaali sahaayak company he jiskaa ekmaatr uddeshy jamaaon ko beemaa cover pradaan karnaa or credit suvidhaon kii guarantee dena he
 However, there are ways through which you can enjoy high deposit insurance cover
 aap apni jamaa raashi ko vibhajit kar sakate hai or ise vibhinn bainkon main rakh sakate hai; ek hi bank main apni jamaa raashi ko alag-alag khaaton main vibhajit karen, jise alag-alag adhikaar or kshamta main rakhaa gaya he
 For example, keep the account as an individual, or a joint account holder, partner of a firm, a director of a company, guardian of a minor, etc
, then all these accounts will be eligible for separate insurance cover of Rs 1 lakh
 
 cover badhayen1993 tak, jamaa beemaa cover niyamit rup se badhaayaa gaya tha

 agle 24 se 48 ghanto tak jammu kashmir ke saath saath himachal ke tamaam ilaakon main baari se bahut baari barfbaari kii ashanka bad gai he

 According to Charan Singh, director of the Meteorological Department, the western disturbance of this time is powerful and it is getting moisture from the Arabian Sea
 arab sagar se mil rahi nami kii vajah se pakistan samet uttar-pashchim bharat ke tamaam ilaakon main barish olavrishti or barfbaari kii ashanka zyada he
